./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createInstance()
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Vulkan Instance..." << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:    if (enableValidationLayers && !checkValidationLayerSupport())
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("Validation layers requested, but not available");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (enableValidationLayers)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        std::cout << "Validation layers enabled" << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // --- Application info ---
./intiVk.cxx:    VkApplicationInfo appInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:    appInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_APPLICATION_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:    appInfo.pApplicationName = "Hello Triangle";
./intiVk.cxx:    appInfo.applicationVersion = VK_MAKE_VERSION(1, 0, 0);
./intiVk.cxx:    appInfo.pEngineName = "No Engine";
./intiVk.cxx:    appInfo.engineVersion = VK_MAKE_VERSION(1, 0, 0);
./intiVk.cxx:    appInfo.apiVersion = VK_API_VERSION_1_1; // Use 1.1 for MoltenVK
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // --- Instance create info ---
./intiVk.cxx:    VkInstanceCreateInfo createInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_INSTANCE_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.pApplicationInfo = &appInfo;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // --- Validation layers ---
./intiVk.cxx:    if (enableValidationLayers)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        createInfo.enabledLayerCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(validationLayers.size());
./intiVk.cxx:        createInfo.ppEnabledLayerNames = validationLayers.data();
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:    else
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        createInfo.enabledLayerCount = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:        createInfo.ppEnabledLayerNames = nullptr;
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // --- Required extensions ---
./intiVk.cxx:    uint32_t glfwExtensionCount = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:    const char **glfwExtensions = glfwGetRequiredInstanceExtensions(&glfwExtensionCount);
./intiVk.cxx:    std::vector<const char *> requiredExtensions(glfwExtensions, glfwExtensions + glfwExtensionCount);
./intiVk.cxx:    requiredExtensions.push_back(VK_KHR_PORTABILITY_ENUMERATION_EXTENSION_NAME);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.flags |= VK_INSTANCE_CREATE_ENUMERATE_PORTABILITY_BIT_KHR;
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.enabledExtensionCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(requiredExtensions.size());
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.ppEnabledExtensionNames = requiredExtensions.data();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // --- Create instance ---
./intiVk.cxx:    if (vkCreateInstance(&createInfo, nullptr, &instance) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create instance!");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // --- Print available extensions ---
./intiVk.cxx:    uint32_t extensionCount = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkEnumerateInstanceExtensionProperties(nullptr, &extensionCount, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:    std::vector<VkExtensionProperties> extensions(extensionCount);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkEnumerateInstanceExtensionProperties(nullptr, &extensionCount, extensions.data());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "available extensions:\n";
./intiVk.cxx:    for (const auto &extension : extensions)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        std::cout << '\t' << extension.extensionName << '\n';
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// finding if VL_LAYERS_KHRONOS_validation is there or not
./intiVk.cxx:bool HelloTriangleApplication::checkValidationLayerSupport()
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    uint32_t layerCount;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkEnumerateInstanceLayerProperties(&layerCount, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::vector<VkLayerProperties> availableLayers(layerCount);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkEnumerateInstanceLayerProperties(&layerCount, availableLayers.data());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    for (const char *layerName : validationLayers)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        bool layerFound = false;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        for (auto &layerPorperties : availableLayers)
./intiVk.cxx:        {
./intiVk.cxx:            if (strcmp(layerName, layerPorperties.layerName) == 0)
./intiVk.cxx:            {
./intiVk.cxx:                layerFound = true;
./intiVk.cxx:                break;
./intiVk.cxx:            }
./intiVk.cxx:        }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        if (!layerFound)
./intiVk.cxx:        {
./intiVk.cxx:            return false;
./intiVk.cxx:        }
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    return true;
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::pickPhysicalDevice()
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "Picking Physical Device..." << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:    physicalDevice = VK_NULL_HANDLE; // this will be implicitly cleanup when VkInstance is destroid(no additoinal cleanup needed)
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    uint32_t deviceCount = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkEnumeratePhysicalDevices(instance, &deviceCount, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (deviceCount == 0)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to find GPUs that support Vulkan");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::vector<VkPhysicalDevice> devices(deviceCount);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkEnumeratePhysicalDevices(instance, &deviceCount, devices.data());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::multimap<int, VkPhysicalDevice> candidates;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    for (const auto &device : devices)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        int score = rateDeviceSuitablity(device);
./intiVk.cxx:        candidates.insert(std::make_pair(score, device));
./intiVk.cxx:        std::cout << "Score: " << score << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (candidates.rbegin()->first > 0)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        physicalDevice = candidates.rbegin()->second;
./intiVk.cxx:        msaaSamples = getMaxUsableSampleCount();
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:    else
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("Failed to find a suitable GPU");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// right now we only allow to use dedicated cards the support geometry shaders
./intiVk.cxx:// bool HelloTriangleApplication::isDeviceSuitable(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:// {
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx://     // this controls which type of GPU to allow
./intiVk.cxx://     return deviceProperties.deviceType == VK_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_TYPE_DISCRETE_GPU && deviceFeatures.geometryShader;
./intiVk.cxx:// }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:int HelloTriangleApplication::rateDeviceSuitablity(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceProperties props;
./intiVk.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures feats;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceProperties(device, &props);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceFeatures(device, &feats);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    int score = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "Device: " << props.deviceName << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // Prefer discrete or integrated GPU
./intiVk.cxx:    if (props.deviceType == VK_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_TYPE_DISCRETE_GPU)
./intiVk.cxx:        score += 10000;
./intiVk.cxx:    else if (props.deviceType == VK_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_TYPE_INTEGRATED_GPU)
./intiVk.cxx:        score += 5000;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // Bigger textures = better
./intiVk.cxx:    score += props.limits.maxImageDimension2D;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // Useful features
./intiVk.cxx:    if (feats.samplerAnisotropy)
./intiVk.cxx:        score += 1000;
./intiVk.cxx:    if (feats.shaderInt64)
./intiVk.cxx:        score += 500;
./intiVk.cxx:    if (feats.wideLines)
./intiVk.cxx:        score += 300;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:#ifdef __APPLE__
./intiVk.cxx:    // Metal backend doesn’t support geometry/tessellation shaders
./intiVk.cxx:    score += 1500;
./intiVk.cxx:#else
./intiVk.cxx:    if (!feats.geometryShader)
./intiVk.cxx:        return 0; // skip if no geometry shader
./intiVk.cxx:#endif
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    return score;
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// Queue -> a line in which a set of commands needs to be executed
./intiVk.cxx:// there maybe multiple types of queues(Graphics, Computem, ...)
./intiVk.cxx:// Queue Family -> Conatains multiple queues for the GPU(Note: A queue family must be homogenous)
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// finding queue families
./intiVk.cxx:HelloTriangleApplication::QueueFamilyIndices HelloTriangleApplication::findQueueFamilies(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    QueueFamilyIndices indices;
./intiVk.cxx:    uint32_t queueFamilyCount = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceQueueFamilyProperties(device, &queueFamilyCount, nullptr); // grts all the queue families supported by the GPU
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::vector<VkQueueFamilyProperties> queueFamilies(queueFamilyCount);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceQueueFamilyProperties(device, &queueFamilyCount, queueFamilies.data());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    int i = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:    for (const auto &queueFamily : queueFamilies)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        if (queueFamily.queueFlags & VK_QUEUE_GRAPHICS_BIT)
./intiVk.cxx:            indices.graphicsFamily = i;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        VkBool32 presentSupport = false;
./intiVk.cxx:        vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceSupportKHR(device, i, surface, &presentSupport);
./intiVk.cxx:        if (presentSupport)
./intiVk.cxx:            indices.presentFamily = i;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        if (indices.isComplete())
./intiVk.cxx:            break;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        i++;
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:    // NOTE: some GPU supports different graphics and presentation queues
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    return indices;
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// Logical device -> A brige between the program and the GPU
./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createLogicalDevice()
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Logical Device..." << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:    // Queue Family Stuff
./intiVk.cxx:    QueueFamilyIndices indices = findQueueFamilies(physicalDevice); // get the required queue families
./intiVk.cxx:    std::vector<VkDeviceQueueCreateInfo> queueCreateInfos;
./intiVk.cxx:    std::set<uint32_t> uniqueQueueFamilies = {indices.graphicsFamily.value(), indices.presentFamily.value()};
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // right now only creating a single queue(can create muliple)
./intiVk.cxx:    float queuePriority = 1.f;
./intiVk.cxx:    for (uint32_t queueFamily : uniqueQueueFamilies) // prepare each queue family
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        VkDeviceQueueCreateInfo queueCreateInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:        queueCreateInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_DEVICE_QUEUE_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:        queueCreateInfo.queueFamilyIndex = queueFamily;
./intiVk.cxx:        queueCreateInfo.queueCount = 1;
./intiVk.cxx:        queueCreateInfo.pQueuePriorities = &queuePriority;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        queueCreateInfos.push_back(queueCreateInfo); // push the queue info in the vector
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // ---- Specifing which feature we wanna use ----
./intiVk.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures deviceFeatures{};
./intiVk.cxx:    deviceFeatures.samplerAnisotropy = VK_TRUE;
./intiVk.cxx:    deviceFeatures.sampleRateShading = VK_TRUE;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // If you're on Vulkan 1.2, use VkPhysicalDeviceVulkan12Features instead:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceVulkan12Features vk12Features{};
./intiVk.cxx:    vk12Features.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_VULKAN_1_2_FEATURES;
./intiVk.cxx:    vk12Features.descriptorIndexing                        = VK_TRUE;
./intiVk.cxx:    vk12Features.shaderSampledImageArrayNonUniformIndexing = VK_TRUE;
./intiVk.cxx:    vk12Features.pNext = nullptr;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDeviceCreateInfo createInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_DEVICE_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.queueCreateInfoCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(queueCreateInfos.size());
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.pQueueCreateInfos = queueCreateInfos.data();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.pEnabledFeatures = &deviceFeatures;
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.pNext = &vk12Features;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:#ifdef __APPLE__
./intiVk.cxx:    deviceExtensions.push_back("VK_KHR_portability_subset");
./intiVk.cxx:#else
./intiVk.cxx:    deviceExtensions.push_back(VK_KHR_SWAPCHAIN_EXTENSION_NAME);
./intiVk.cxx:#endif
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    deviceExtensions.push_back(VK_EXT_DESCRIPTOR_INDEXING_EXTENSION_NAME);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.enabledExtensionCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(deviceExtensions.size());
./intiVk.cxx:    createInfo.ppEnabledExtensionNames = deviceExtensions.data();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // Device specific validation layers
./intiVk.cxx:    if (enableValidationLayers)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        createInfo.enabledLayerCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(validationLayers.size());
./intiVk.cxx:        createInfo.ppEnabledLayerNames = validationLayers.data();
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:    else
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        createInfo.enabledLayerCount = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (vkCreateDevice(physicalDevice, &createInfo, nullptr, &device) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("Faild to create logical device");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // ---- retrive the queues and store them into the class members ----
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetDeviceQueue(device, indices.graphicsFamily.value(), 0, &graphicsQueue);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetDeviceQueue(device, indices.presentFamily.value(), 0, &presentQueue);
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// this is never called because I have rateDeviceSutablity
./intiVk.cxx:// this is just redundent
./intiVk.cxx:bool HelloTriangleApplication::isDeviceSuitable(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    QueueFamilyIndices indices = findQueueFamilies(device);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    bool extensionsSupported = checkDeviceExtensionSupport(device);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceDescriptorIndexingFeatures indexingSupport{};
./intiVk.cxx:    indexingSupport.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_DESCRIPTOR_INDEXING_FEATURES;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures2 features2{};
./intiVk.cxx:    features2.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_FEATURES_2;
./intiVk.cxx:    features2.pNext = &indexingSupport;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceFeatures2(physicalDevice, &features2);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (!indexingSupport.shaderSampledImageArrayNonUniformIndexing)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("Device does not support non-uniform texture indexing!");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    bool swapChainAdequate = false;
./intiVk.cxx:    if (extensionsSupported)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        SwapChainSupportDetails swapChainSupport = querySwapChainSupport(device);
./intiVk.cxx:        swapChainAdequate = !swapChainSupport.formats.empty() && !swapChainSupport.presentModes.empty();
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    return indices.isComplete() && extensionsSupported && swapChainAdequate;
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:bool HelloTriangleApplication::checkDeviceExtensionSupport(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    // ---- counting the number of extensions ----
./intiVk.cxx:    uint32_t extensionCount;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkEnumerateDeviceExtensionProperties(device, nullptr, &extensionCount, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::vector<VkExtensionProperties> availableExtansions(extensionCount);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkEnumerateDeviceExtensionProperties(device, nullptr, &extensionCount, availableExtansions.data()); // all the required extensions are now retrived
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::set<std::string> requiredExtensions(deviceExtensions.begin(), deviceExtensions.end());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    for (const auto &extension : availableExtansions)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        requiredExtensions.erase(extension.extensionName);
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // if all the required extensions are supported then the 'requiredExtension' vector is empty
./intiVk.cxx:    // which returns true
./intiVk.cxx:    return requiredExtensions.empty();
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// Swapchain -> A queue of images presented to the screen in a sequence
./intiVk.cxx:// Draw to an offscreen -> present it to the current window -> repeat
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// This function asks the GPU about the capablitie of the SwapChain that this GPU has
./intiVk.cxx:HelloTriangleApplication::SwapChainSupportDetails HelloTriangleApplication::querySwapChainSupport(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    SwapChainSupportDetails details;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // ---- Get the capabilities ----
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceCapabilitiesKHR(device, surface, &details.capabilities);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // ---- get the format ----
./intiVk.cxx:    uint32_t formatCount;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceFormatsKHR(device, surface, &formatCount, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (formatCount != 0)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        details.formats.resize(formatCount);
./intiVk.cxx:        vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceFormatsKHR(device, surface, &formatCount, details.formats.data());
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // ---- get the presentation mode(vsync, mailbox ...) ----
./intiVk.cxx:    uint32_t presentModeCount;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfacePresentModesKHR(device, surface, &presentModeCount, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (presentModeCount != 0)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfacePresentModesKHR(device, surface, &presentModeCount, details.presentModes.data());
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    return details;
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:VkSurfaceFormatKHR HelloTriangleApplication::chooseSwapSurfaceFormat(const std::vector<VkSurfaceFormatKHR> &availableFormats)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        for (const auto &availableFormat : availableFormats)
./intiVk.cxx:        {
./intiVk.cxx:            if (availableFormat.format == VK_FORMAT_B8G8R8A8_SRGB && availableFormat.colorSpace == VK_COLORSPACE_SRGB_NONLINEAR_KHR)
./intiVk.cxx:            {
./intiVk.cxx:                return availableFormat;
./intiVk.cxx:            }
./intiVk.cxx:        }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        return availableFormats.at(0);
./intiVk.cxx:    }

./intiVk.cxx:// Extent defines the resolution of the image
./intiVk.cxx:// MacOS has a fixed extent while other windowing systems have a varible extent which is clamped to the window bounds
./intiVk.cxx:// also High-DPI displays like Apple Liquid Retina displays have to be configure in a sepreate way
./intiVk.cxx:VkExtent2D HelloTriangleApplication::chooseSwapExtent(const VkSurfaceCapabilitiesKHR &capabilities)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:#ifdef __APPLE__
./intiVk.cxx:    // MoltenVK on macOS (Retina-safe)
./intiVk.cxx:    int width, height;
./intiVk.cxx:    glfwGetFramebufferSize(_window, &width, &height);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkExtent2D actualExtent = {
./intiVk.cxx:        static_cast<uint32_t>(width),
./intiVk.cxx:        static_cast<uint32_t>(height)};
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    return actualExtent; // Always use framebuffer size on Retina
./intiVk.cxx:#else
./intiVk.cxx:    // Metal IE: the size is predifined and is not UINT 32 max. therefore, use the size provided by the system
./intiVk.cxx:    if (capabilities.currentExtent.width != std::numeric_limits<uint32_t>::max())
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        return capabilities.currentExtent;
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:    // The surface does not have a fixed size and you must create it by yourself
./intiVk.cxx:    else
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        int width, height;
./intiVk.cxx:        glfwGetFramebufferSize(_window, &width, &height);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        VkExtent2D actualExtent =
./intiVk.cxx:            {
./intiVk.cxx:                static_cast<uint32_t>(width),
./intiVk.cxx:                static_cast<uint32_t>(height)};
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        actualExtent.width = std::clamp(actualExtent.width, capabilities.minImageExtent.width, capabilities.maxImageExtent.width);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        actualExtent.height = std::clamp(actualExtent.height, capabilities.minImageExtent.height, capabilities.maxImageExtent.height);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        return actualExtent;
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:#endif
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// here we are using a staging buffer which is accisible by the CPU and then afterwards copying the contents of the staging buffer to the vertex buffer
./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createVertexBuffer()
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Vertex Buffer..." << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDeviceSize bufferSize = sizeof(vertices[0]) * vertices.size();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkBuffer stagingBuffer;
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDeviceMemory stagingBufferMemory;
./intiVk.cxx:    // TX
./intiVk.cxx:    createBuffer(bufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT | VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_CACHED_BIT, stagingBuffer, stagingBufferMemory);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // filling in the vertex buffer
./intiVk.cxx:    void *data;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkMapMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory, 0, bufferSize, 0, &data);
./intiVk.cxx:    memcpy(data, vertices.data(), (size_t)bufferSize);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkUnmapMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // creating the actul VBO and setting it up so the it is the destionation of the transfer source
./intiVk.cxx:    // TX
./intiVk.cxx:    createBuffer(bufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT | VK_BUFFER_USAGE_VERTEX_BUFFER_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_DEVICE_LOCAL_BIT, vertexBuffer, vertexBufferMemory);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // but we still have to copy the memory contents manully
./intiVk.cxx:    copyBuffer(stagingBuffer, vertexBuffer, bufferSize);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(device, stagingBuffer, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createDescriptorSets()
./intiVk.cxx:{

./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    descriptorSets.resize(MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT);
./intiVk.cxx:    if (vkAllocateDescriptorSets(device, &allocInfo, descriptorSets.data()) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate descriptor sets!");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    updateDescriptorSets(texture);
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::updateDescriptorSets(u_Texture &texture)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    for (size_t i = 0; i < MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT; i++)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        VkDescriptorBufferInfo bufferInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:        bufferInfo.buffer = uniformBuffers[i];
./intiVk.cxx:        bufferInfo.offset = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:        bufferInfo.range = sizeof(UniformBufferObject);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        VkDescriptorImageInfo imageInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:        imageInfo.imageLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL;
./intiVk.cxx:        imageInfo.imageView = texture.textureImageView;
./intiVk.cxx:        imageInfo.sampler = texture.textureSampler;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        std::vector<VkDescriptorImageInfo> imageInfos(NUM_DESCRIPTOR_COUNT_FOR_UI_TEXTURES);
./intiVk.cxx:        for (uint32_t i = 0; i < NUM_DESCRIPTOR_COUNT_FOR_UI_TEXTURES; i++)
./intiVk.cxx:        {
./intiVk.cxx:            imageInfos[i].imageLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL;
./intiVk.cxx:            imageInfos[i].imageView = uiTextures[i].textureImageView; // your VkImageView array
./intiVk.cxx:            imageInfos[i].sampler = uiTextures[i].textureSampler;
./intiVk.cxx:        }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        std::array<VkWriteDescriptorSet, 3> descriptorWrites{};
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[0].sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_WRITE_DESCRIPTOR_SET;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[0].dstSet = descriptorSets[i];
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[0].dstBinding = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[0].dstArrayElement = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[0].descriptorType = VK_DESCRIPTOR_TYPE_UNIFORM_BUFFER;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[0].descriptorCount = 1;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[0].pBufferInfo = &bufferInfo;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[1].sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_WRITE_DESCRIPTOR_SET;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[1].dstSet = descriptorSets[i];
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[1].dstBinding = 1;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[1].dstArrayElement = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[1].descriptorType = VK_DESCRIPTOR_TYPE_COMBINED_IMAGE_SAMPLER;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[1].descriptorCount = 1;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[1].pImageInfo = &imageInfo;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[2].sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_WRITE_DESCRIPTOR_SET;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[2].dstSet = descriptorSets[i];
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[2].dstBinding = 2;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[2].dstArrayElement = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[2].descriptorType = VK_DESCRIPTOR_TYPE_COMBINED_IMAGE_SAMPLER;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[2].descriptorCount = NUM_DESCRIPTOR_COUNT_FOR_UI_TEXTURES;
./intiVk.cxx:        descriptorWrites[2].pImageInfo = imageInfos.data();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:        vkUpdateDescriptorSets(device, static_cast<uint32_t>(descriptorWrites.size()), descriptorWrites.data(), 0, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createDescriptorSetLayout()
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Descriptor Set Layout..." << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDescriptorSetLayoutBinding uboLayoutBinding{};
./intiVk.cxx:    uboLayoutBinding.binding = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:    uboLayoutBinding.descriptorCount = 1;
./intiVk.cxx:    uboLayoutBinding.descriptorType = VK_DESCRIPTOR_TYPE_UNIFORM_BUFFER;
./intiVk.cxx:    uboLayoutBinding.pImmutableSamplers = nullptr;
./intiVk.cxx:    uboLayoutBinding.stageFlags = VK_SHADER_STAGE_VERTEX_BIT;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDescriptorSetLayoutBinding samplerLayoutBinding{};
./intiVk.cxx:    samplerLayoutBinding.binding = 1;
./intiVk.cxx:    samplerLayoutBinding.descriptorCount = 1;
./intiVk.cxx:    samplerLayoutBinding.descriptorType = VK_DESCRIPTOR_TYPE_COMBINED_IMAGE_SAMPLER;
./intiVk.cxx:    samplerLayoutBinding.pImmutableSamplers = nullptr;
./intiVk.cxx:    samplerLayoutBinding.stageFlags = VK_SHADER_STAGE_FRAGMENT_BIT;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDescriptorSetLayoutBinding uiTexturesBinding{};
./intiVk.cxx:    uiTexturesBinding.binding = 2;
./intiVk.cxx:    uiTexturesBinding.descriptorType = VK_DESCRIPTOR_TYPE_COMBINED_IMAGE_SAMPLER;
./intiVk.cxx:    uiTexturesBinding.descriptorCount = NUM_DESCRIPTOR_COUNT_FOR_UI_TEXTURES;
./intiVk.cxx:    uiTexturesBinding.stageFlags = VK_SHADER_STAGE_FRAGMENT_BIT;
./intiVk.cxx:    uiTexturesBinding.pImmutableSamplers = nullptr;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDescriptorBindingFlags bindingFlags = VK_DESCRIPTOR_BINDING_PARTIALLY_BOUND_BIT;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDescriptorSetLayoutBindingFlagsCreateInfo flagsInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:    flagsInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_DESCRIPTOR_SET_LAYOUT_BINDING_FLAGS_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:    flagsInfo.bindingCount = 3;
./intiVk.cxx:    flagsInfo.pBindingFlags = &bindingFlags;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    std::array<VkDescriptorSetLayoutBinding, 3> bindings = {uboLayoutBinding, samplerLayoutBinding, uiTexturesBinding};
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDescriptorSetLayoutCreateInfo layoutInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:    layoutInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_DESCRIPTOR_SET_LAYOUT_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:    layoutInfo.bindingCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(bindings.size());
./intiVk.cxx:    layoutInfo.pBindings = bindings.data();
./intiVk.cxx:    layoutInfo.pNext = nullptr;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (vkCreateDescriptorSetLayout(device, &layoutInfo, nullptr, &descriptorSetLayout) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create descriptor set layout!");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::copyBuffer(VkBuffer srcBuffer, VkBuffer dstBuffer, VkDeviceSize size)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkBufferCopy copyRegion{};
./intiVk.cxx:    copyRegion.size = size;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkCmdCopyBuffer(commandBuffer, srcBuffer, dstBuffer, 1, &copyRegion);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    endSingleTimeCommands(commandBuffer);
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:uint32_t HelloTriangleApplication::findMemoryType(uint32_t typeFilter, VkMemoryPropertyFlags properties)
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties memProperties;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties(physicalDevice, &memProperties);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < memProperties.memoryTypeCount; i++)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        if ((typeFilter & (1 << i)) && (memProperties.memoryTypes[i].propertyFlags & properties) == properties)
./intiVk.cxx:        {
./intiVk.cxx:            return i;
./intiVk.cxx:        }
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to find suitable memory type!");
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// A command buffer is a queue of commands to send to the GPU
./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createCommandBuffers()
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Command Buffers..." << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    commandBuffers.resize(MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkCommandBufferAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:    allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:    allocInfo.commandPool = commandPool;
./intiVk.cxx:    allocInfo.level = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_LEVEL_PRIMARY;
./intiVk.cxx:    allocInfo.commandBufferCount = (uint32_t)commandBuffers.size();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (vkAllocateCommandBuffers(device, &allocInfo, commandBuffers.data()) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate command buffers");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createSyncObject()
./intiVk.cxx:{
./intiVk.cxx:    // 1️⃣ Per-frame semaphores for acquiring images
./intiVk.cxx:    imageAvailableSemaphores.resize(MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // 2️⃣ Per-swapchain-image semaphores for rendering completion
./intiVk.cxx:    renderFinishedSemaphores.resize(swapChainImages.size());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // 3️⃣ Fences to limit frames in flight
./intiVk.cxx:    inFlightFences.resize(MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkSemaphoreCreateInfo semaphoreInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:    semaphoreInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SEMAPHORE_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkFenceCreateInfo fenceInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:    fenceInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_FENCE_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:    fenceInfo.flags = VK_FENCE_CREATE_SIGNALED_BIT; // start signaled
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // Create per-frame semaphores and fences
./intiVk.cxx:    for (size_t i = 0; i < MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT; i++)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        if (vkCreateSemaphore(device, &semaphoreInfo, nullptr, &imageAvailableSemaphores[i]) != VK_SUCCESS ||
./intiVk.cxx:            vkCreateFence(device, &fenceInfo, nullptr, &inFlightFences[i]) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVk.cxx:        {
./intiVk.cxx:            throw std::runtime_error("failed to create semaphore or fence!");
./intiVk.cxx:        }
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // Create per-swapchain-image render-finished semaphores
./intiVk.cxx:    for (size_t i = 0; i < swapChainImages.size(); i++)
./intiVk.cxx:    {
./intiVk.cxx:        if (vkCreateSemaphore(device, &semaphoreInfo, nullptr, &renderFinishedSemaphores[i]) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVk.cxx:        {
./intiVk.cxx:            throw std::runtime_error("failed to create renderFinished semaphore!");
./intiVk.cxx:        }
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:}

./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:// Telling vulkan how to pass data to the vertex shader once it's been uploaded into the GPU
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:VkVertexInputBindingDescription Vertex::getBindingDescription()
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:{
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkVertexInputBindingDescription bindingDescription{};
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // A vertex binding describes at which rate to load data from memory throughout the verticies.
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // It specifies the number of bytes between data entries and whether to move to the next data entery after each vertex or after each instance.
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.binding = 0; // binding index to zero
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.stride = sizeof(Vertex);
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.inputRate = VK_VERTEX_INPUT_RATE_VERTEX; // advance to the next input per vertex
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    return bindingDescription;
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:}
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:// this structure describies how to handle vertex input
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:// each attribute required its own description
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:std::array<VkVertexInputAttributeDescription, 4> Vertex::getAttributeDescriptions()
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:{
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    std::array<VkVertexInputAttributeDescription, 4> attributeDescriptions{};
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].binding = 0;                         // same as getBindingDescription
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].location = 0;                        // directly co-relates to 'layout(location = 0)'
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32_SFLOAT; // vec3
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].offset = offsetof(Vertex, pos);
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:

./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].location = 1;
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32_SFLOAT; // vec3

./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[2].location = 2;
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[2].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32_SFLOAT;
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[2].offset = offsetof(Vertex, texCoord);
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:

./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[3].format = VK_FORMAT_R32_SFLOAT;
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[3].offset = offsetof(Vertex, brightness);
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // Formats
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    //  float -> VK_FORMAT_R32_SFLOAT
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    //  vec2  -> VK_FORMAT_R32G32_SFLOAT
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    //  vec3  -> VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32_SFLOAT
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    //  vec4  -> VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32A32_SFLOAT
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // ivec2  -> VK_FORMAT_R32G32_SINT
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // uvec4  -> VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32A32_UINT
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // double -> VK_FORMAT_R64_SFLOAT
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    return attributeDescriptions;
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:}

./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::createBuffer(VulkanContext vkContext, VkDeviceSize size, VkBufferUsageFlags usage, VkMemoryPropertyFlags properties, VkBuffer &buffer, VkDeviceMemory &bufferMemory)
./Textures.cxx:{
./Textures.cxx:    VkBufferCreateInfo bufferInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:    bufferInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_BUFFER_CREATE_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:    bufferInfo.size = size;
./Textures.cxx:    bufferInfo.usage = usage;
./Textures.cxx:    bufferInfo.sharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_EXCLUSIVE;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    if (vkCreateBuffer(vkContext.device, &bufferInfo, nullptr, &buffer) != VK_SUCCESS)
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create buffer!");
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkMemoryRequirements memRequirements;
./Textures.cxx:    vkGetBufferMemoryRequirements(vkContext.device, buffer, &memRequirements);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkMemoryAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:    allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_MEMORY_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:    allocInfo.allocationSize = memRequirements.size;
./Textures.cxx:    uint32_t typeFilter = memRequirements.memoryTypeBits;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties memProperties;
./Textures.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties(vkContext.physicalDevice, &memProperties);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < memProperties.memoryTypeCount; i++)
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        if ((typeFilter & (1 << i)) && (memProperties.memoryTypes[i].propertyFlags & properties) == properties)
./Textures.cxx:        {
./Textures.cxx:            allocInfo.memoryTypeIndex = i;
./Textures.cxx:            goto _ok;
./Textures.cxx:        }
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to find suitable memory type!");
./Textures.cxx:    _ok:;
./Textures.cxx:    if (vkAllocateMemory(vkContext.device, &allocInfo, nullptr, &bufferMemory) != VK_SUCCESS)
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate buffer memory!");
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkBindBufferMemory(vkContext.device, buffer, bufferMemory, 0);
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:uint32_t u_Texture::findMemoryType(uint32_t typeFilter, VkMemoryPropertyFlags properties)
./Textures.cxx:{
./Textures.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties memProperties;
./Textures.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties(physicalDevice, &memProperties);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < memProperties.memoryTypeCount; i++)
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        if ((typeFilter & (1 << i)) && (memProperties.memoryTypes[i].propertyFlags & properties) == properties)
./Textures.cxx:        {
./Textures.cxx:            return i;
./Textures.cxx:        }
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to find suitable memory type!");
./Textures.cxx:}

./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::createTextureImage()
./Textures.cxx:{
./Textures.cxx:    int texWidth, texHeight, texChannels;
./Textures.cxx:    stbi_uc *pixels = stbi_load(texturePath.c_str(), &texWidth, &texHeight, &texChannels, STBI_rgb_alpha);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    mipLevels = static_cast<uint32_t>(std::floor(std::log2(std::max(texWidth, texHeight)))) + 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkDeviceSize imageSize = texWidth * texHeight * 4; // 4 -> r,g,b,a
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    if (!pixels)
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("Failed to load image");
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkBuffer stagingBuffer;
./Textures.cxx:    VkDeviceMemory stagingBufferMemory;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    createBuffer(imageSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT | VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_COHERENT_BIT, stagingBuffer, stagingBufferMemory);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    void *data;
./Textures.cxx:    vkMapMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory, 0, imageSize, 0, &data);
./Textures.cxx:    memcpy(data, pixels, static_cast<size_t>(imageSize));
./Textures.cxx:    vkUnmapMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    stbi_image_free(pixels);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    createImage(texWidth, texHeight, VK_SAMPLE_COUNT_1_BIT, mipLevels, VK_FORMAT_R8G8B8A8_SRGB, VK_IMAGE_TILING_OPTIMAL, VK_IMAGE_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT | VK_IMAGE_USAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT | VK_IMAGE_USAGE_SAMPLED_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_DEVICE_LOCAL_BIT, textureImage, textureImageMemory);
./Textures.cxx:    transitionImageLayout(textureImage, VK_FORMAT_R8G8B8A8_SRGB, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL, mipLevels);
./Textures.cxx:    copyBufferToImage(stagingBuffer, textureImage, static_cast<uint32_t>(texWidth), static_cast<uint32_t>(texHeight));
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    generateMipmaps(textureImage, VK_FORMAT_R8G8B8A8_SRGB, texWidth, texHeight, mipLevels);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(device, stagingBuffer, nullptr);
./Textures.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Textures.cxx:}

./Textures.cxx:VkCommandBuffer u_Texture::beginSingleTimeCommands()
./Textures.cxx:{
./Textures.cxx:    VkCommandBufferAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:    allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:    allocInfo.level = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_LEVEL_PRIMARY;
./Textures.cxx:    allocInfo.commandPool = commandPool;
./Textures.cxx:    allocInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer;
./Textures.cxx:    vkAllocateCommandBuffers(device, &allocInfo, &commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkCommandBufferBeginInfo beginInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:    beginInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_BEGIN_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:    beginInfo.flags = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_USAGE_ONE_TIME_SUBMIT_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkBeginCommandBuffer(commandBuffer, &beginInfo);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    return commandBuffer;
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::endSingleTimeCommands(VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer)
./Textures.cxx:{
./Textures.cxx:    vkEndCommandBuffer(commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkSubmitInfo submitInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:    submitInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SUBMIT_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:    submitInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:    submitInfo.pCommandBuffers = &commandBuffer;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkQueueSubmit(graphicsQueue, 1, &submitInfo, VK_NULL_HANDLE);
./Textures.cxx:    vkQueueWaitIdle(graphicsQueue);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkFreeCommandBuffers(device, commandPool, 1, &commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:// before copying the image to the buffer we need to set it into the right layout
./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::transitionImageLayout(VkImage image, VkFormat format, VkImageLayout oldLayout, VkImageLayout newLayout, uint32_t mipLevels)
./Textures.cxx:{
./Textures.cxx:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkImageMemoryBarrier barrier{};
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_MEMORY_BARRIER;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.oldLayout = oldLayout;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.newLayout = newLayout;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    // We are not transfering queue family ownership rn!!!
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.srcQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.dstQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.image = image;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.levelCount = mipLevels;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.srcAccessMask = 0; // todo
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.dstAccessMask = 0; // todo
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkPipelineStageFlags sourceStage;
./Textures.cxx:    VkPipelineStageFlags destinationStage;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    if (oldLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED && newLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL)
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.srcAccessMask = 0;
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:        sourceStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TOP_OF_PIPE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:        destinationStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:    else if (oldLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL && newLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL)
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_SHADER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:        sourceStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:        destinationStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_FRAGMENT_SHADER_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:    else
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        throw std::invalid_argument("unsupported layout transition!");
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkCmdPipelineBarrier(
./Textures.cxx:        commandBuffer,
./Textures.cxx:        sourceStage, destinationStage,
./Textures.cxx:        0,
./Textures.cxx:        0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:        0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:        1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    endSingleTimeCommands(commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::copyBufferToImage(VkBuffer buffer, VkImage image, uint32_t width, uint32_t height)
./Textures.cxx:{
./Textures.cxx:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkBufferImageCopy region{};
./Textures.cxx:    region.bufferOffset = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    region.bufferRowLength = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    region.bufferImageHeight = 0;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    region.imageSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    region.imageSubresource.mipLevel = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    region.imageSubresource.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    region.imageSubresource.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    region.imageOffset = {0, 0, 0};
./Textures.cxx:    region.imageExtent = {width, height, 1};
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkCmdCopyBufferToImage(commandBuffer, buffer, image, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL, 1, &region);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    endSingleTimeCommands(commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::generateMipmaps(VkImage image, VkFormat imageFormat, int32_t texWidth, int32_t texHeight, uint32_t mipLevels)
./Textures.cxx:{
./Textures.cxx:    // Check if image format supports linear blitting
./Textures.cxx:    VkFormatProperties formatProperties;
./Textures.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceFormatProperties(physicalDevice, imageFormat, &formatProperties);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    if (!(formatProperties.optimalTilingFeatures & VK_FORMAT_FEATURE_SAMPLED_IMAGE_FILTER_LINEAR_BIT))
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("texture image format does not support linear blitting!");
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkImageMemoryBarrier barrier{};
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_MEMORY_BARRIER;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.image = image;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.srcQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.dstQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.levelCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    int32_t mipWidth = texWidth;
./Textures.cxx:    int32_t mipHeight = texHeight;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    for (uint32_t i = 1; i < mipLevels; i++)
./Textures.cxx:    {
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = i - 1;
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.oldLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.newLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:        barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:        vkCmdPipelineBarrier(commandBuffer,
./Textures.cxx:                             VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT, VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT, 0,
./Textures.cxx:                             0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:                             0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:                             1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:        VkImageBlit blit{};
./Textures.cxx:        blit.srcOffsets[0] = {0, 0, 0};
./Textures.cxx:        blit.srcOffsets[1] = {mipWidth, mipHeight, 1};
./Textures.cxx:        blit.srcSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:        blit.srcSubresource.mipLevel = i - 1;
./Textures.cxx:        blit.srcSubresource.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:        blit.srcSubresource.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:        blit.dstOffsets[0] = {0, 0, 0};
./Textures.cxx:        blit.dstOffsets[1] = {mipWidth > 1 ? mipWidth / 2 : 1, mipHeight > 1 ? mipHeight / 2 : 1, 1};
./Textures.cxx:        blit.dstSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:        blit.dstSubresource.mipLevel = i;
./Textures.cxx:        blit.dstSubresource.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:        blit.dstSubresource.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:        vkCmdBlitImage(commandBuffer,
./Textures.cxx:                       image, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL,
./Textures.cxx:                       image, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL,

./Player.cxx:void Player::handlePlayerMovement(UniformBufferObject &UBO, VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent, Event &event)
./Player.cxx:{
./Player.cxx:    constexpr float JUMP_TIMESCALE_MS = 200.f;
./Player.cxx:    constexpr float JUMP_END_THRESHOLD = 4.5f;
./Player.cxx:    constexpr float JUMP_SCALE = .5f;
./Player.cxx:    constexpr float GRAVITY = 1.61f;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    camera->updateUBO(UBO, swapChainExtent, event);
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    glm::vec3 playerCoords = camera->cameraPos;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    aabb.max = playerCoords + glm::vec3(.15f, .15f, 0);
./Player.cxx:    aabb.min = playerCoords - glm::vec3(.15f, .15f, 2);
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    // ground collision
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    Voxel *voxel = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal(BlockCoordinates{floor(playerCoords.x), floor(playerCoords.y), floor(playerCoords.z - 2)});
./Player.cxx:    if (voxel && voxel->getBlockType() != AIR)
./Player.cxx:    {
./Player.cxx:        std::cout << "Player AABB: "
./Player.cxx:                  << "min(" << aabb.min.x << ", " << aabb.min.y << ", " << aabb.min.z << "), "
./Player.cxx:                  << "max(" << aabb.max.x << ", " << aabb.max.y << ", " << aabb.max.z << ")\n";
./Player.cxx:        std::cout << "Voxel AABB: "
./Player.cxx:                  << "min(" << voxel->aabb.min.x << ", " << voxel->aabb.min.y << ", " << voxel->aabb.min.z << "), "
./Player.cxx:                  << "max(" << voxel->aabb.max.x << ", " << voxel->aabb.max.y << ", " << voxel->aabb.max.z << ")\n";
./Player.cxx:        // std::cout << "Voxel Coords: "
./Player.cxx:        //           << "min(" << voxel->aabb.min.x << ", " << voxel->aabb.min.y << ", " << voxel->aabb.min.z << "), "
./Player.cxx:        //           << "max(" << voxel->aabb.max.x << ", " << voxel->aabb.max.y << ", " << voxel->aabb.max.z << ")\n";
./Player.cxx:        if ((aabb.max.x > voxel->aabb.min.x && aabb.min.x < voxel->aabb.max.x) &&
./Player.cxx:            (aabb.max.y > voxel->aabb.min.y && aabb.min.y < voxel->aabb.max.y) &&
./Player.cxx:            (aabb.max.z > voxel->aabb.min.z && aabb.min.z < voxel->aabb.max.z))
./Player.cxx:        {
./Player.cxx:            std::cout << "SKAHKHKS" << std::endl;
./Player.cxx:        }
./Player.cxx:    }
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_LEFT_SHIFT))
./Player.cxx:        camera->cameraPos.z -= camera->speed;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    return;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    auto now = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();
./Player.cxx:    long long now_ms = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::milliseconds>(
./Player.cxx:                           now.time_since_epoch())
./Player.cxx:                           .count();
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    if (playerState.onGround && ((now_ms - jumpStartTime) > 250))
./Player.cxx:    {
./Player.cxx:        playerState.inJump = false;
./Player.cxx:    }
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    if (playerState.onGround && !playerState.inJump && event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_SPACE))
./Player.cxx:    {
./Player.cxx:        playerState.inJump = true;
./Player.cxx:        jumpStartTime = now_ms;
./Player.cxx:    }
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    if (playerState.inJump)
./Player.cxx:    {
./Player.cxx:        float te = (now_ms - jumpStartTime) / JUMP_TIMESCALE_MS;
./Player.cxx:        camera->cameraPos.z += JUMP_SCALE * jump((te)) * camera->speed;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:        if (te > JUMP_END_THRESHOLD)
./Player.cxx:        {
./Player.cxx:            playerState.inJump = false;
./Player.cxx:        }
./Player.cxx:        std::cout << te << std::endl;
./Player.cxx:    }
./Player.cxx:    else if (!playerState.onGround)
./Player.cxx:    {
./Player.cxx:        camera->cameraPos.z -= camera->speed / GRAVITY;
./Player.cxx:    }
./Player.cxx:}

./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::drawFrame()
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:{
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 1️⃣ Wait for previous frame to finish
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkWaitForFences(device, 1, &inFlightFences[currentFrame], VK_TRUE, UINT64_MAX);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkResetFences(device, 1, &inFlightFences[currentFrame]);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 2️⃣ Acquire an image from the swapchain
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    uint32_t imageIndex;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkResult res = vkAcquireNextImageKHR(
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        device,
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        swapChain,
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        UINT64_MAX,
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        imageAvailableSemaphores[currentFrame], // still per-frame
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        VK_NULL_HANDLE,
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        &imageIndex);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    if (res != VK_SUCCESS && res != VK_SUBOPTIMAL_KHR)
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    {
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to acquire swap chain image!");
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    }
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkResetCommandBuffer(commandBuffers[currentFrame], 0); // or VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_RESET_RELEASE_RESOURCES_BIT
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    terrain.value().handelDirtyChunks();
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    updateUniformBuffer(currentFrame);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    recordCommandBuffer(commandBuffers[currentFrame], imageIndex);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 5️⃣ Submit the command buffer to the graphics queue
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkSubmitInfo submitInfo{};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SUBMIT_INFO;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkSemaphore waitSemaphores[] = {imageAvailableSemaphores[currentFrame]};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkPipelineStageFlags waitStages[] = {VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OUTPUT_BIT};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.waitSemaphoreCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.pWaitSemaphores = waitSemaphores;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.pWaitDstStageMask = waitStages;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.pCommandBuffers = &commandBuffers[currentFrame];
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // ✅ Use renderFinishedSemaphore per swapchain image
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkSemaphore signalSemaphores[] = {renderFinishedSemaphores[imageIndex]};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.signalSemaphoreCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.pSignalSemaphores = signalSemaphores;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    if (vkQueueSubmit(graphicsQueue, 1, &submitInfo, inFlightFences[currentFrame]) != VK_SUCCESS)
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to submit draw command buffer!");
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 6️⃣ Present the image
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkPresentInfoKHR presentInfo{};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PRESENT_INFO_KHR;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.waitSemaphoreCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.pWaitSemaphores = signalSemaphores;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkSwapchainKHR swapChains[] = {swapChain};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.swapchainCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.pSwapchains = swapChains;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.pImageIndices = &imageIndex;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkQueuePresentKHR(presentQueue, &presentInfo);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 7️⃣ Advance frame
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    currentFrame = (currentFrame + 1) % MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT;

./intiVK2.cxx:// In a swapchain we only use color images as that is all the is need to simply draw on the screen
./intiVK2.cxx:// Depth buffers and other stuff is handled in other places
./intiVK2.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createSwapChain()
./intiVK2.cxx:{
./intiVK2.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Swap Chain..." << std::endl;
./intiVK2.cxx:    // ---- get the swapchain capabilities
./intiVK2.cxx:    SwapChainSupportDetails swapChainSupport = querySwapChainSupport(physicalDevice);
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // pick the best options
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkSurfaceFormatKHR surfaceFormat = chooseSwapSurfaceFormat(swapChainSupport.formats);
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkPresentModeKHR presentMode = chooseSwapPresentMode(swapChainSupport.presentModes);
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkExtent2D extent = chooseSwapExtent(swapChainSupport.capabilities);
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // ---- save the format and extent ----
./intiVK2.cxx:    swapChainImageFormat = surfaceFormat.format;
./intiVK2.cxx:    swapChainExtent = extent;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // add one to allow triple buffering
./intiVK2.cxx:    // Metal limits the max to 3 so only +1 one is allowed while NVIDIA and AMD has no limits
./intiVK2.cxx:    uint32_t imageCount = swapChainSupport.capabilities.minImageCount + 1;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // Check to not exeed the maximum
./intiVK2.cxx:    // 0 is a special number meaning that there is not upper limit
./intiVK2.cxx:    if (swapChainSupport.capabilities.maxImageCount > 0 && imageCount > swapChainSupport.capabilities.maxImageCount)
./intiVK2.cxx:    {
./intiVK2.cxx:        imageCount = swapChainSupport.capabilities.maxImageCount;
./intiVK2.cxx:    }
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkSwapchainCreateInfoKHR createInfo{};
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SWAPCHAIN_CREATE_INFO_KHR;
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.surface = surface; // surface
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // ---- Image settings ----
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.minImageCount = imageCount;
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.imageFormat = surfaceFormat.format;
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.imageColorSpace = surfaceFormat.colorSpace;
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.imageExtent = extent;
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.imageArrayLayers = 1;
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.imageUsage = VK_IMAGE_USAGE_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_BIT; // for post VFX use VK_IMAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // ---- graphics and present queue familiy equality check
./intiVK2.cxx:    QueueFamilyIndices indices = findQueueFamilies(physicalDevice);
./intiVK2.cxx:    uint32_t queueFamilyIndices[] = {indices.graphicsFamily.value(), indices.presentFamily.value()};
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // If not same then use concurrent which means that we dont have to worry about the manual ownership
./intiVK2.cxx:    // If same then use exclusive which is faster
./intiVK2.cxx:    if (indices.graphicsFamily != indices.presentFamily)
./intiVK2.cxx:    {
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.imageSharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_CONCURRENT;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.queueFamilyIndexCount = 2;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.pQueueFamilyIndices = queueFamilyIndices;
./intiVK2.cxx:    }
./intiVK2.cxx:    else
./intiVK2.cxx:    {
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.imageSharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_EXCLUSIVE;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.queueFamilyIndexCount = 0;     // Optional
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.pQueueFamilyIndices = nullptr; // Optional
./intiVK2.cxx:    }
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // how to transform the present
./intiVK2.cxx:    // IE: tell vulkan how to handle rotations. We just use what the windowing system provides
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.preTransform = swapChainSupport.capabilities.currentTransform;
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.compositeAlpha = VK_COMPOSITE_ALPHA_OPAQUE_BIT_KHR; // how shall this window blend with other windows
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.presentMode = presentMode;
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.clipped = VK_TRUE; // don't care about the pixels that are not seen on the screen
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    createInfo.oldSwapchain = VK_NULL_HANDLE; // later stuff
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    if (vkCreateSwapchainKHR(device, &createInfo, nullptr, &swapChain) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVK2.cxx:    {
./intiVK2.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create swap chain!");
./intiVK2.cxx:    }
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // ---- Retrive the images ----
./intiVK2.cxx:    vkGetSwapchainImagesKHR(device, swapChain, &imageCount, nullptr);
./intiVK2.cxx:    swapChainImages.resize(imageCount);
./intiVK2.cxx:    vkGetSwapchainImagesKHR(device, swapChain, &imageCount, swapChainImages.data());
./intiVK2.cxx:}
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:// Images views: VkImage is just raw memory. Image views provide the GPU with all the neseccary context and information to present the data correctly
./intiVK2.cxx:// We did specify in the swapchain what formats and options to use, then why an image view?
./intiVK2.cxx:// Because a VkImage by itself proved no indication of the location and size of the contents
./intiVK2.cxx:// An Image view providies those important information to the GPU
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createImageViews()
./intiVK2.cxx:{
./intiVK2.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Image Views..." << std::endl;
./intiVK2.cxx:    swapChainImageViews.resize(swapChainImages.size());
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    for (size_t i = 0; i < swapChainImages.size(); i++)
./intiVK2.cxx:    {
./intiVK2.cxx:        VkImageViewCreateInfo createInfo{};
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_VIEW_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.image = swapChainImages[i];
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:        // specifing how shall the images be interpreted
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.viewType = VK_IMAGE_VIEW_TYPE_2D;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.format = swapChainImageFormat;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:        // mapping the color channels to defaults
./intiVK2.cxx:        // VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY → use the original channel layout.
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.components.r = VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.components.g = VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.components.b = VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.components.a = VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:        // specifing how shall the images be use(their purpose)
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT; // color targets
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = 0;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.subresourceRange.levelCount = 1;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./intiVK2.cxx:        createInfo.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:        if (vkCreateImageView(device, &createInfo, nullptr, &swapChainImageViews[i]) != VK_SUCCESS)
./intiVK2.cxx:        {
./intiVK2.cxx:            throw std::runtime_error("Failed to create image views");
./intiVK2.cxx:        }
./intiVK2.cxx:    }
./intiVK2.cxx:}
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:// Render pass
./intiVK2.cxx:// It tells vulkan what attachment to use
./intiVK2.cxx:// How to use
./intiVK2.cxx:// Layout transitions
./intiVK2.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createRenderPass()
./intiVK2.cxx:{
./intiVK2.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Render Pass..." << std::endl;
./intiVK2.cxx:    // ---- describing what rescources we will be using ----
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkAttachmentDescription depthAttachment{};
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachment.format = VK_FORMAT_D32_SFLOAT;
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachment.samples = msaaSamples;
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachment.loadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_CLEAR;
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachment.storeOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachment.stencilLoadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachment.stencilStoreOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachment.initialLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED;
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachment.finalLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_DEPTH_STENCIL_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkAttachmentReference depthAttachmentRef{};
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachmentRef.attachment = 1;
./intiVK2.cxx:    depthAttachmentRef.layout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_DEPTH_STENCIL_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkAttachmentDescription colorAttachment{};
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachment.format = swapChainImageFormat;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachment.samples = msaaSamples;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachment.loadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_CLEAR;   // what to do with the framebuffer after the render pass has started
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachment.storeOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_STORE; // what to do with the memory(store it in the vram or not)
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    // don't care about the stencil
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachment.stencilLoadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachment.stencilStoreOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachment.initialLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachment.finalLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkAttachmentReference colorAttachmentRef{};
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentRef.attachment = 0; // IDX to the attachment
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentRef.layout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkAttachmentDescription colorAttachmentResolve{};
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolve.format = swapChainImageFormat;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolve.samples = VK_SAMPLE_COUNT_1_BIT;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolve.loadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolve.storeOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_STORE;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolve.stencilLoadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolve.stencilStoreOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolve.initialLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolve.finalLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_PRESENT_SRC_KHR;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkAttachmentReference colorAttachmentResolveRef{};
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolveRef.attachment = 2;
./intiVK2.cxx:    colorAttachmentResolveRef.layout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkSubpassDescription subpass{};
./intiVK2.cxx:    subpass.pipelineBindPoint = VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS; // alternative is compute
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    subpass.colorAttachmentCount = 1;
./intiVK2.cxx:    subpass.pColorAttachments = &colorAttachmentRef;
./intiVK2.cxx:    subpass.pDepthStencilAttachment = &depthAttachmentRef;
./intiVK2.cxx:    subpass.pResolveAttachments = &colorAttachmentResolveRef;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    std::array<VkAttachmentDescription, 3> attachments = {colorAttachment, depthAttachment, colorAttachmentResolve};
./intiVK2.cxx:    VkRenderPassCreateInfo renderPassInfo{};

./intiVK2.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::loadModel()
./intiVK2.cxx:{
./intiVK2.cxx:    tinyobj::attrib_t attrib;
./intiVK2.cxx:    std::vector<tinyobj::shape_t> shapes;
./intiVK2.cxx:    std::vector<tinyobj::material_t> materials;
./intiVK2.cxx:    std::string err, warn;
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    if (!tinyobj::LoadObj(&attrib, &shapes, &materials, &warn, &err, MODEL_PATH.c_str()))
./intiVK2.cxx:    {
./intiVK2.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error(err);
./intiVK2.cxx:    }
./intiVK2.cxx:    if (warn.empty() == false)
./intiVK2.cxx:    {
./intiVK2.cxx:        std::cout << "WARN: " << warn << std::endl;
./intiVK2.cxx:    }
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    std::unordered_map<Vertex, uint32_t> uniqueVertices{};
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:    for (const auto &shape : shapes)
./intiVK2.cxx:    {
./intiVK2.cxx:        for (const auto &index : shape.mesh.indices)
./intiVK2.cxx:        {
./intiVK2.cxx:            Vertex vertex{};
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:            vertex.pos = {
./intiVK2.cxx:                attrib.vertices[3 * index.vertex_index + 0],
./intiVK2.cxx:                attrib.vertices[3 * index.vertex_index + 1],
./intiVK2.cxx:                attrib.vertices[3 * index.vertex_index + 2]};
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:            vertex.texCoord = {
./intiVK2.cxx:                attrib.texcoords[2 * index.texcoord_index + 0],
./intiVK2.cxx:                1.0f - attrib.texcoords[2 * index.texcoord_index + 1]};
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:            vertex.color = {1.0f, 1.0f, 1.0f};
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:            if (uniqueVertices.count(vertex) == 0)
./intiVK2.cxx:            {
./intiVK2.cxx:                uniqueVertices[vertex] = static_cast<uint32_t>(vertices.size());
./intiVK2.cxx:                vertices.push_back(vertex);
./intiVK2.cxx:            }
./intiVK2.cxx:
./intiVK2.cxx:            indices.push_back(uniqueVertices[vertex]);
./intiVK2.cxx:        }
./intiVK2.cxx:    }
./intiVK2.cxx:}

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.pColorBlendState = &colorBlending;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // pipelineInfo.pDynamicState = &dynamic_state;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.layout = pipelineLayout;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.subpass = 0;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    if (vkCreateGraphicsPipelines(device, VK_NULL_HANDLE, 1, &pipelineInfo, nullptr, &graphicsPipeline) != VK_SUCCESS)
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    {
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create graphics pipeline!");
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    }
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vkDestroyShaderModule(device, fragShaderModule, nullptr);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vkDestroyShaderModule(device, vertShaderModule, nullptr);

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:VkVertexInputBindingDescription RayPoints::getBindingDescription()
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:{
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkVertexInputBindingDescription bindingDescription{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // A vertex binding describes at which rate to load data from memory throughout the verticies.
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // It specifies the number of bytes between data entries and whether to move to the next data entery after each vertex or after each instance.
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.binding = 0; // binding index to zero
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.stride = sizeof(RayPoints);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.inputRate = VK_VERTEX_INPUT_RATE_VERTEX; // advance to the next input per vertex
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    return bindingDescription;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:}
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:std::array<VkVertexInputAttributeDescription, 2> RayPoints::getAttributeDescriptions()
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:{
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    std::array<VkVertexInputAttributeDescription, 2> attributeDescriptions{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].binding = 0;                         // same as getBindingDescription
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].location = 0;                        // directly co-relates to 'layout(location = 0)'
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32_SFLOAT; // vec3
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].offset = offsetof(RayPoints, pos);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].binding = 0;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].location = 1;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32_SFLOAT; // vec3
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].offset = offsetof(RayPoints, color);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    return attributeDescriptions;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:}
