./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:void Chunk::populateBlocks()
./Chunk.cxx:{
./Chunk.cxx:    voxels.reserve(16 * 16 * 256);
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    for (int z = 0; z < 256; z++)
./Chunk.cxx:    {
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; x++)
./Chunk.cxx:        {
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; y++)
./Chunk.cxx:            {
./Chunk.cxx:                int blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                if (z <= 50)
./Chunk.cxx:                    blockType = STONE;
./Chunk.cxx:                else if (z <= 64)
./Chunk.cxx:                    blockType = GRASS;
./Chunk.cxx:                else
./Chunk.cxx:                    blockType = AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                voxels.emplace_back(vkContext, BlockType(blockType));
./Chunk.cxx:                voxels.back().setType(BlockType(blockType));
./Chunk.cxx:                voxels.back().transform.position = {
./Chunk.cxx:                    (float)x + 0.5f,
./Chunk.cxx:                    (float)y + 0.5f,
./Chunk.cxx:                    (float)z + 0.5f};
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:    }
./Chunk.cxx:}
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:bool Chunk::isFaceVisible(int x, int y, int z)
./Chunk.cxx:{
./Chunk.cxx:    Voxel *v = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal({x + chunkOffsetX * 16,
./Chunk.cxx:                                              y + chunkOffsetY * 16,
./Chunk.cxx:                                              z});
./Chunk.cxx:    return v == nullptr || v->getBlockType() == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:}
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:void Chunk::genMesh(bool useChunkMesh)
./Chunk.cxx:{
./Chunk.cxx:    std::vector<Vertex> vertices;
./Chunk.cxx:    std::vector<uint32_t> indices;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    vertices.reserve(16 * 16 * 64 * 4);
./Chunk.cxx:    indices.reserve(16 * 16 * 64 * 6);
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    // Each face wound CCW when viewed from OUTSIDE (normal = cross(e1, e2) points outward)
./Chunk.cxx:    // Verified: cross(v1-v0, v2-v0) must point in the face's outward normal direction
./Chunk.cxx:    static const FaceDef faces[6] = {
./Chunk.cxx:        // Top (+Z)
./Chunk.cxx:        {{{-0.5f, -0.5f, 0.5f}, {0.5f, -0.5f, 0.5f}, {0.5f, 0.5f, 0.5f}, {-0.5f, 0.5f, 0.5f}},
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         1.0f,
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         1},
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        // Bottom (-Z)
./Chunk.cxx:        {{{-0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f}, {-0.5f, 0.5f, -0.5f}, {0.5f, 0.5f, -0.5f}, {0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f}},
./Chunk.cxx:         1,
./Chunk.cxx:         0.5f,
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         -1},
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        // Front (+Y)
./Chunk.cxx:        {{{-0.5f, 0.5f, -0.5f}, {-0.5f, 0.5f, 0.5f}, {0.5f, 0.5f, 0.5f}, {0.5f, 0.5f, -0.5f}},
./Chunk.cxx:         2,
./Chunk.cxx:         0.75f,
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         1,
./Chunk.cxx:         0},
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        // Back (-Y)
./Chunk.cxx:        {{{0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f}, {0.5f, -0.5f, 0.5f}, {-0.5f, -0.5f, 0.5f}, {-0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f}},
./Chunk.cxx:         3,
./Chunk.cxx:         0.85f,
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         -1,
./Chunk.cxx:         0},
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        // Right (+X)
./Chunk.cxx:        {{{0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f}, {0.5f, 0.5f, -0.5f}, {0.5f, 0.5f, 0.5f}, {0.5f, -0.5f, 0.5f}},
./Chunk.cxx:         4,
./Chunk.cxx:         0.7f,
./Chunk.cxx:         1,
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         0},
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        // Left (-X)
./Chunk.cxx:        {{{-0.5f, 0.5f, -0.5f}, {-0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f}, {-0.5f, -0.5f, 0.5f}, {-0.5f, 0.5f, 0.5f}},
./Chunk.cxx:         5,
./Chunk.cxx:         0.8f,
./Chunk.cxx:         -1,
./Chunk.cxx:         0,
./Chunk.cxx:         0},
./Chunk.cxx:    };
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    auto blockColor = [](BlockType type) -> glm::vec3
./Chunk.cxx:    {
./Chunk.cxx:        switch (type)
./Chunk.cxx:        {
./Chunk.cxx:        case STONE:
./Chunk.cxx:            return {0.5f, 0.5f, 0.5f};
./Chunk.cxx:        case GRASS:
./Chunk.cxx:            return {0.4f, 0.8f, 0.3f};
./Chunk.cxx:        default:
./Chunk.cxx:            return {1.0f, 1.0f, 1.0f};
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:    };
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    for (int z = 0; z < 256; z++)
./Chunk.cxx:    {
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; x++)
./Chunk.cxx:        {
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; y++)
./Chunk.cxx:            {
./Chunk.cxx:                const int idx = z * 256 + x * 16+ y;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                const BlockType type = voxels.at(idx).getBlockType();
./Chunk.cxx:                const int *faceTexture = voxels.at(idx).faceTexture;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                if (type == AIR)
./Chunk.cxx:                    continue;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                const glm::vec3 color = blockColor(type);
./Chunk.cxx:                const glm::vec3 origin = voxels.at(idx).transform.position;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                for (const FaceDef &face : faces)
./Chunk.cxx:                {
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!isFaceVisible(x + face.dx, y + face.dy, z + face.dz))
./Chunk.cxx:                        continue;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    const uint32_t base = static_cast<uint32_t>(vertices.size());
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    vertices.push_back({origin + face.corners[0], color, glm::vec2(faceTexture[face.tileOffset], 0), face.light});
./Chunk.cxx:                    vertices.push_back({origin + face.corners[1], color, glm::vec2(faceTexture[face.tileOffset], 1), face.light});
./Chunk.cxx:                    vertices.push_back({origin + face.corners[2], color, glm::vec2(faceTexture[face.tileOffset], 2), face.light});
./Chunk.cxx:                    vertices.push_back({origin + face.corners[3], color, glm::vec2(faceTexture[face.tileOffset], 3), face.light});
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    indices.insert(indices.end(), {base, base + 1, base + 2, base + 2, base + 3, base});
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:    }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    if (useChunkMesh)
./Chunk.cxx:    {
./Chunk.cxx:        chunkMesh.vertices = std::move(vertices);
./Chunk.cxx:        chunkMesh.indices = std::move(indices);
./Chunk.cxx:    }
./Chunk.cxx:    else
./Chunk.cxx:    {
./Chunk.cxx:        backMesh.vertices = std::move(vertices);
./Chunk.cxx:        backMesh.indices = std::move(indices);
./Chunk.cxx:    }
./Chunk.cxx:}
./Chunk.cxx:

./Chunk.cxx:    genMesh();
./Chunk.cxx:    chunkMesh.createVertexBuffer();
./Chunk.cxx:    chunkMesh.createIndexBuffer();
./Chunk.cxx:    backMesh.createVertexBuffer();
./Chunk.cxx:    backMesh.createIndexBuffer();

./Chunk.cxx:void Chunk::swapMesh()
./Chunk.cxx:{
./Chunk.cxx:    chunkMesh.vertices = std::move(backMesh.vertices);
./Chunk.cxx:    chunkMesh.indices = std::move(backMesh.indices);
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    backMesh.vertices.clear();
./Chunk.cxx:    backMesh.indices.clear();
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    chunkMesh.updateVertexBuffer();
./Chunk.cxx:    chunkMesh.updateIndexBuffer();
./Chunk.cxx:}

./Chunk.cxx:void Chunk::draw(VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer, VkPipelineLayout pipelineLayout, VkPipeline graphicsPipeline,
./Chunk.cxx:                 std::vector<VkDescriptorSet> &descriptorSets, uint32_t currentFrame, VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent)
./Chunk.cxx:{
./Chunk.cxx:    VkBuffer vertexBuffers[] = {chunkMesh.vertexBuffer};
./Chunk.cxx:    VkDeviceSize offsets[] = {0};
./Chunk.cxx:    vkCmdBindVertexBuffers(commandBuffer, 0, 1, vertexBuffers, offsets);
./Chunk.cxx:    vkCmdBindIndexBuffer(commandBuffer, chunkMesh.indexBuffer, 0, VK_INDEX_TYPE_UINT32);
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    PushConstantC1 c1;
./Chunk.cxx:    c1.data = glm::translate(glm::mat4(1.f), glm::vec3(chunkOffsetX * 16, chunkOffsetY * 16, 0));
./Chunk.cxx:    vkCmdPushConstants(commandBuffer, pipelineLayout, VK_SHADER_STAGE_VERTEX_BIT, 0, sizeof(PushConstantC1), &c1);
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    vkCmdBindDescriptorSets(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS, pipelineLayout,
./Chunk.cxx:                            0, 1, &(descriptorSets[currentFrame]), 0, nullptr);
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    vkCmdDrawIndexed(commandBuffer, static_cast<uint32_t>(chunkMesh.indices.size()), 1, 0, 0, 0);
./Chunk.cxx:}

./GameObjectPool.cxx:Chunk *GameObjectPool::getChunk(int chunkX, int chunkY)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:{
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    if(!terrain)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        return nullptr;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    for (auto &chunk : terrain->chunks)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    {
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        if (chunk.chunkOffsetX == chunkX && chunk.chunkOffsetY == chunkY)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:            return &chunk;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    }
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    return nullptr;

./GameObjectPool.cxx:Voxel *GameObjectPool::getVoxelGlobal(BlockCoordinates globalCoords)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:{
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    if (!terrain)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        return nullptr;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int chunkX = globalCoords.x >> 4;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int chunkY = globalCoords.y >> 4;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int localX = globalCoords.x & 15;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int localY = globalCoords.y & 15;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int localZ = globalCoords.z;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    // Bounds check before touching any chunk
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    if (localZ < 0 || localZ >= 256)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        return nullptr;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    for (auto &chunk : terrain->chunks)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    {
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        if (chunk.chunkOffsetX == chunkX && chunk.chunkOffsetY == chunkY)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        {
./GameObjectPool.cxx:            // Access voxels directly — never call getVoxelChunkLocal here
./GameObjectPool.cxx:            int idx = localX + localY * 16 + localZ * 256;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:            return &chunk.voxels[idx];
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        }
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    }
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    return nullptr;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:}

./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:void UIRenderPipeline::createGraphicsPipeline()
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:{
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating UI Graphics Pipeline..." << std::endl;
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    auto vertShaderCode = readFile("shaders/simple_shader_ui_v.spv");
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    auto fragShaderCode = readFile("shaders/simple_shader_ui_f.spv");
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    VkShaderModule vertShaderModule = createShaderModule(vertShaderCode);
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    VkShaderModule fragShaderModule = createShaderModule(fragShaderCode);
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    // shaderStageCreation
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineShaderStageCreateInfo vertShaderStageInfo{};
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    vertShaderStageInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_SHADER_STAGE_CREATE_INFO;
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    vertShaderStageInfo.stage = VK_SHADER_STAGE_VERTEX_BIT; // telling vulkan 'which stage must this shader go'
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    vertShaderStageInfo.module = vertShaderModule;
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    vertShaderStageInfo.pName = "main";
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineShaderStageCreateInfo fragShaderStageInfo{};
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    fragShaderStageInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_SHADER_STAGE_CREATE_INFO;
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    fragShaderStageInfo.stage = VK_SHADER_STAGE_FRAGMENT_BIT;
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    fragShaderStageInfo.module = fragShaderModule;
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    fragShaderStageInfo.pName = "main";
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineShaderStageCreateInfo shaderStages[] = {vertShaderStageInfo, fragShaderStageInfo};
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    auto bindingDescription = UIVertex::getBindingDescription();
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    auto attributeDescriptions = UIVertex::getAttributeDescriptions();
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:

./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:VkVertexInputBindingDescription UIVertex::getBindingDescription()
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:{
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    VkVertexInputBindingDescription bindingDescription{};
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    // A vertex binding describes at which rate to load data from memory throughout the verticies.
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    // It specifies the number of bytes between data entries and whether to move to the next data entery after each vertex or after each instance.
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.binding = 0; // binding index to zero
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.stride = sizeof(UIVertex);
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.inputRate = VK_VERTEX_INPUT_RATE_VERTEX; // advance to the next input per vertex
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    return bindingDescription;
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:}
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:

./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:{

./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].binding = 0;                         // same as getBindingDescription
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].location = 0;                        // directly co-relates to 'layout(location = 0)'
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32_SFLOAT; // vec3
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].offset = offsetof(UIVertex, pos);
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].binding = 0;

./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32_SFLOAT; // vec2

./Chunk.h:struct BlockCoordinatesHash
./Chunk.h:{
./Chunk.h:    std::size_t operator()(const BlockCoordinates &b) const noexcept
./Chunk.h:    {
./Chunk.h:        std::size_t h1 = std::hash<int>{}(b.x);
./Chunk.h:        std::size_t h2 = std::hash<int>{}(b.y);
./Chunk.h:        std::size_t h3 = std::hash<int>{}(b.z);
./Chunk.h:
./Chunk.h:        return h1 ^ (h2 << 1) ^ (h3 << 2);
./Chunk.h:    }
./Chunk.h:};

./GraphicsPipeline.h:namespace std {
./GraphicsPipeline.h:    template<>
./GraphicsPipeline.h:    struct hash<Vertex> {
./GraphicsPipeline.h:        size_t operator()(Vertex const& vertex) const {
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            size_t seed = 0;
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            auto hashCombine = [&seed](auto const& v) {
./GraphicsPipeline.h:                seed ^= std::hash<float>()(v)
./GraphicsPipeline.h:                      + 0x9e3779b97f4a7c15
./GraphicsPipeline.h:                      + (seed << 6)
./GraphicsPipeline.h:                      + (seed >> 2);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            };
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.x);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.y);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.z);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.r);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.g);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.b);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.texCoord.x);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.texCoord.y);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            return seed;
./GraphicsPipeline.h:        }
./GraphicsPipeline.h:    };
./GraphicsPipeline.h:}

./utils.cxx:#include "utils.h"
./utils.cxx:#include <stdexcept>
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:void utils::createBuffer(VkDeviceSize size, VkBufferUsageFlags usage, VkMemoryPropertyFlags properties, VkBuffer &buffer, VkDeviceMemory &bufferMemory, VulkanContext &vkContext)
./utils.cxx:{
./utils.cxx:    VkBufferCreateInfo bufferInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    bufferInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_BUFFER_CREATE_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    bufferInfo.size = size;
./utils.cxx:    bufferInfo.usage = usage;
./utils.cxx:    bufferInfo.sharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_EXCLUSIVE;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    if (vkCreateBuffer(vkContext.device, &bufferInfo, nullptr, &buffer) != VK_SUCCESS)
./utils.cxx:    {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    VkMemoryRequirements memRequirements;
./utils.cxx:    vkGetBufferMemoryRequirements(vkContext.device, buffer, &memRequirements);
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    VkMemoryAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_MEMORY_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.allocationSize = memRequirements.size;
./utils.cxx:    uint32_t typeFilter = memRequirements.memoryTypeBits;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties memProperties;
./utils.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties(vkContext.physicalDevice, &memProperties);
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < memProperties.memoryTypeCount; i++)
./utils.cxx:    {
./utils.cxx:        if ((typeFilter & (1 << i)) && (memProperties.memoryTypes[i].propertyFlags & properties) == properties)
./utils.cxx:        {
./utils.cxx:            allocInfo.memoryTypeIndex = i;
./utils.cxx:            goto _ok;
./utils.cxx:        }
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to find suitable memory type!");
./utils.cxx:    _ok:;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    if (vkAllocateMemory(vkContext.device, &allocInfo, nullptr, &bufferMemory) != VK_SUCCESS)
./utils.cxx:    {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate buffer memory!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    vkBindBufferMemory(vkContext.device, buffer, bufferMemory, 0);
./utils.cxx:}
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:void utils::copyBuffer(VkBuffer srcBuffer, VkBuffer dstBuffer, VkDeviceSize size, VulkanContext &vkContext)
./utils.cxx:{
./utils.cxx:    // 1. Create a temporary command buffer
./utils.cxx:    VkCommandBufferAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.level = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_LEVEL_PRIMARY;
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.commandPool = vkContext.commandPool; // your command pool
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer;
./utils.cxx:    if (vkAllocateCommandBuffers(vkContext.device, &allocInfo, &commandBuffer) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 2. Begin the command buffer
./utils.cxx:    VkCommandBufferBeginInfo beginInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    beginInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_BEGIN_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    beginInfo.flags = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_USAGE_ONE_TIME_SUBMIT_BIT;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    if (vkBeginCommandBuffer(commandBuffer, &beginInfo) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to begin command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 3. Define the copy region
./utils.cxx:    VkBufferCopy copyRegion{};
./utils.cxx:    copyRegion.srcOffset = 0; // optional
./utils.cxx:    copyRegion.dstOffset = 0; // optional
./utils.cxx:    copyRegion.size = size;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 4. Record the copy command
./utils.cxx:    vkCmdCopyBuffer(commandBuffer, srcBuffer, dstBuffer, 1, &copyRegion);
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 5. End the command buffer
./utils.cxx:    if (vkEndCommandBuffer(commandBuffer) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to end command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 6. Submit the command buffer and wait
./utils.cxx:    VkSubmitInfo submitInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    submitInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SUBMIT_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    submitInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./utils.cxx:    submitInfo.pCommandBuffers = &commandBuffer;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    if (vkQueueSubmit(vkContext.graphicsQueue, 1, &submitInfo, VK_NULL_HANDLE) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to submit copy command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:    vkQueueWaitIdle(vkContext.graphicsQueue);
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 7. Free the temporary command buffer
./utils.cxx:    vkFreeCommandBuffers(vkContext.device, vkContext.commandPool, 1, &commandBuffer);
./utils.cxx:}

./Event.h:
./Event.h:class KeyTracker {
./Event.h:    std::unordered_map<int, bool> prevState;
./Event.h:public:
./Event.h:    // Call this once per frame AFTER all key checks
./Event.h:    void update(auto* event, std::initializer_list<int> keys) {
./Event.h:        for (int key : keys)
./Event.h:            prevState[key] = event->getKeyPressed(key);
./Event.h:    }
./Event.h:
./Event.h:    bool justPressed(auto* event, int key) {
./Event.h:        return event->getKeyPressed(key) && !prevState[key];
./Event.h:    }
./Event.h:
./Event.h:    bool justReleased(auto* event, int key) {
./Event.h:        return !event->getKeyPressed(key) && prevState[key];
./Event.h:    }
./Event.h:};
./Event.h:
./Event.h:class Event
./Event.h:{
./Event.h:private:
./Event.h:    GLFWwindow &window;

./Event.h:
./Event.h:    double dt;
./Event.h:
./Event.h:    double mouseX, mouseY;
./Event.h:    Event(GLFWwindow &window);

./Event.h:    static void mouseButtonCallback(GLFWwindow *window, int button, int action, int mods);

./Camera.cxx:void Camera::getHitInfo(HitInfo &hitInfo)
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:{
./Camera.cxx:    float stepSize = 0.1f;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    glm::vec3 rayOriginCR = gePositionInWorldCoords();
./Camera.cxx:    glm::vec3 rayDirCR = forwardCR;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    float maxDistanceCR = 5.0f; // Max ray distance
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    for (float t = 0.0f; t < maxDistanceCR; t += stepSize)
./Camera.cxx:    {
./Camera.cxx:        glm::vec3 point = rayOriginCR + rayDirCR * t;
./Camera.cxx:        BlockCoordinates blockCoords{
./Camera.cxx:            static_cast<int>(floor(point.x)),
./Camera.cxx:            static_cast<int>(floor(point.y)),
./Camera.cxx:            static_cast<int>(floor(point.z))};
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:        Voxel *voxel = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal(blockCoords);
./Camera.cxx:        if (voxel && voxel->getBlockType() != AIR)
./Camera.cxx:        {
./Camera.cxx:            hitInfo.blockCoords = blockCoords;
./Camera.cxx:            hitInfo.hitVoxel = voxel;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:            break;
./Camera.cxx:        }
./Camera.cxx:    }
./Camera.cxx:}

./Camera.cxx:void Camera::updateUBO(UniformBufferObject &UBO,
./Camera.cxx:                       VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent,
./Camera.cxx:                       Event &event)
./Camera.cxx:{
./Camera.cxx:    static double lastX = event.mouseX;
./Camera.cxx:    static double lastY = event.mouseY;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    float dt = event.dt * 0.001f;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    double dx = lastX - event.mouseX;
./Camera.cxx:    double dy = lastY - event.mouseY;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    lastX = event.mouseX;
./Camera.cxx:    lastY = event.mouseY;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    float sensitivity = 0.1f;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    yaw += dx * sensitivity;
./Camera.cxx:    pitch += dy * sensitivity;
./Camera.cxx:    pitch = glm::clamp(pitch, -89.9f, 89.9f);
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    // Z-up forward vector from yaw/pitch
./Camera.cxx:    forwardCR.x = cos(glm::radians(yaw)) * cos(glm::radians(pitch));
./Camera.cxx:    forwardCR.y = sin(glm::radians(yaw)) * cos(glm::radians(pitch));
./Camera.cxx:    forwardCR.z = sin(glm::radians(pitch));
./Camera.cxx:    forwardCR = glm::normalize(forwardCR);
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    glm::vec3 worldUp(0.0f, 0.0f, 1.0f); // Z-up
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    glm::vec3 forwardFlat = glm::normalize(glm::vec3(forwardCR.x, forwardCR.y, 0.0f));
./Camera.cxx:    glm::vec3 right = glm::normalize(glm::cross(worldUp, forwardFlat));
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    speed = 15.81f * dt;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_W))
./Camera.cxx:        cameraPos += forwardFlat * speed;
./Camera.cxx:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_S))
./Camera.cxx:        cameraPos -= forwardFlat * speed;
./Camera.cxx:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_A))
./Camera.cxx:        cameraPos -= -right * speed;
./Camera.cxx:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_D))
./Camera.cxx:        cameraPos += -right * speed;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    UBO.view = glm::lookAt(cameraPos, cameraPos + forwardCR, worldUp);
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    UBO.proj = glm::perspective(
./Camera.cxx:        glm::radians(90.0f),
./Camera.cxx:        swapChainExtent.width / (float)swapChainExtent.height,
./Camera.cxx:        0.025f,
./Camera.cxx:        1000.0f);
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    UBO.proj[1][1] *= -1;
./Camera.cxx:}
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:// Camera space: 1 unit = 10 voxels
./Camera.cxx:glm::vec3 Camera::gePositionInWorldCoords() { return cameraPos; }

./Camera.cxx:{
./Camera.cxx:    cameraRay.cleanup();
./Camera.cxx:

./Camera.cxx:{
./Camera.cxx:

./Camera.cxx:    cameraRay.transform.position.z -= .1f;
./Camera.cxx:    cameraRay.direction = forwardCR;

./Terrain.cxx:#include "Terrain.h"
./Terrain.cxx:#include <iostream>

./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:Terrain::Terrain(VulkanContext &vkContext, GameObjectPool &gameObjectPool) : vkContext{vkContext}, gameObjectPool{gameObjectPool}
./Terrain.cxx:{
./Terrain.cxx:}
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:void Terrain::generateChunks()
./Terrain.cxx:{
./Terrain.cxx:    TIMER_START(GENERATE_CHUNKS);
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:    // Pass 1 — populate all chunks into the pool first
./Terrain.cxx:    for (int x = -RENDER_DISTANCE; x < RENDER_DISTANCE; x++)
./Terrain.cxx:        for (int y = -RENDER_DISTANCE; y < RENDER_DISTANCE; y++)
./Terrain.cxx:        {
./Terrain.cxx:            chunks.emplace_back(vkContext, gameObjectPool);
./Terrain.cxx:            chunks.back().setOffset(x, y);
./Terrain.cxx:            chunks.back().populateBlocks();
./Terrain.cxx:        }
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:    // Pass 2 — all neighbours now exist, cross-chunk culling works
./Terrain.cxx:    for (auto &chunk : chunks)
./Terrain.cxx:        chunk.buildChunkMesh();
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:    TIMER_END(GENERATE_CHUNKS);
./Terrain.cxx:}
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:void Terrain::draw(VkCommandBuffer cmdBuffer, VkPipelineLayout pipelineLayout, VkPipeline graphicsPipeline, std::vector<VkDescriptorSet> &descriptorSets, uint32_t currentFrame, VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent)
./Terrain.cxx:{
./Terrain.cxx:    for (auto &&chunk : chunks)
./Terrain.cxx:    {
./Terrain.cxx:        chunk.draw(cmdBuffer, pipelineLayout, graphicsPipeline, descriptorSets, currentFrame, swapChainExtent);
./Terrain.cxx:    }
./Terrain.cxx:}
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:void Terrain::updateChunkMesh(int chunkX, int chunkY)
./Terrain.cxx:{
./Terrain.cxx:    int idx = chunkIndex(chunkX, chunkY);
./Terrain.cxx:    if(idx < 0 || idx >= chunks.size())
./Terrain.cxx:    {
./Terrain.cxx:        std::cerr << "Invalid chunk coordinates: (" << chunkX << ", " << chunkY << ")" << std::endl;
./Terrain.cxx:        return;
./Terrain.cxx:    }
./Terrain.cxx:    chunks.at(idx).dirty = true;
./Terrain.cxx:    chunks.at(idx).updateChunkMesh();
./Terrain.cxx:}
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:void Terrain::handelDirtyChunks()
./Terrain.cxx:{
./Terrain.cxx:    for (auto &chunk : chunks)
./Terrain.cxx:    {
./Terrain.cxx:        if (chunk.dirty)
./Terrain.cxx:        {
./Terrain.cxx:            chunk.swapMesh();
./Terrain.cxx:            chunk.dirty = false;
./Terrain.cxx:        }
./Terrain.cxx:    }
./Terrain.cxx:}
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:void Terrain::cleanup()
./Terrain.cxx:{
./Terrain.cxx:    for (auto &&c : chunks)
./Terrain.cxx:    {
./Terrain.cxx:        c.cleanup();

./RayMesher.cxx:void RayMesher::draw(VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer, VkPipelineLayout pipelineLayout, VkPipeline graphicsPipeline, std::vector<VkDescriptorSet> &descriptorSets, uint32_t currentFrame, VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent, PushConstantC1 &c1)

./RayMesher.cxx:    VkBuffer vertexBuffers[] = {vertexBuffer};
./RayMesher.cxx:    VkDeviceSize offsets[] = {0};
./RayMesher.cxx:

./RayMesher.cxx:

./RayMesher.cxx:

./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkCmdBindDescriptorSets(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS, pipelineLayout,
./RayMesher.cxx:                            0, 1, &(descriptorSets[currentFrame]), 0, nullptr);
./RayMesher.cxx:

./UIRenderPipeline.h:
./UIRenderPipeline.h:namespace std {
./UIRenderPipeline.h:    template<>
./UIRenderPipeline.h:    struct hash<UIVertex> {
./UIRenderPipeline.h:        size_t operator()(UIVertex const& vertex) const {
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            size_t seed = 0;
./UIRenderPipeline.h:
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            auto hashCombine = [&seed](auto const& v) {
./UIRenderPipeline.h:                seed ^= std::hash<float>()(v)
./UIRenderPipeline.h:                      + 0x9e3779b97f4a7c15
./UIRenderPipeline.h:                      + (seed << 6)
./UIRenderPipeline.h:                      + (seed >> 2);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            };
./UIRenderPipeline.h:
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.x);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.y);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.z);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.uv.r);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.uv.g);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            return seed;
./UIRenderPipeline.h:        }
./UIRenderPipeline.h:    };
./UIRenderPipeline.h:}
